########################
# ITA OOB Events #
########################

#####################################################################################
# ALLOW historical ITA OOB Events (HQ, divisions, brigades creations or upgrades)	#
#####################################################################################
country_event = {

	id = 33492
		
	trigger = {
		tag = ITA
		date = 1936.1.5
		not = { has_country_flag = ITA_historical_OOB_yes }
		not = { has_country_flag = ITA_historical_OOB_no }
	}
	
	title = "EVTNAME33492"
	desc = "EVTDESC33492"
	picture = "ITAevent33408"

	
	option = {
		name = "Allow the events" # ok
		set_country_flag = ITA_historical_OOB_yes
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = "unique_ITA_units"
			duration = 3000
		}
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		supplies = -5000
	}
	option = {
		name = "No Thanks"  # no
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = "no_ITA_units"
			duration = 3000
		}
		set_country_flag = ITA_historical_OOB_no
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
	}
}



# Send the 7a Divisione CC. NN. 'Cirene' in Africa
country_event = {
	id = 33401

	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {
		tag = ITA
		has_country_flag = ITA_historical_OOB_yes
		date = 1936.4.2
		manpower = 14
		supplies = 1000
	}
	
	title = "EVTNAME33401"
	desc = "EVTDESC33401"
	picture = "ITAevent33401"
	
	option = {
		name = "Yes, let's mobilize this division!"

        OMG = {
			any_country = {
				limit = { tag = ITA has_country_flag = BlackICE
                        check_variable = { which = "BaseIC" value = 1 }
                        not = { check_variable = { which = "BaseIC" value = 150 } }
				}
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = "10IC_Unit_spawn_penalty_125_V"
					duration = 110
				}	
				load_oob = ITA/ITA_7a_Div_CCNN.txt
			}
		}
        OMG = {
			any_country = {
				limit = { tag = ITA has_country_flag = BlackICE

	id = 33408

		has_country_flag = ITA_historical_OOB_yes
		date = 1938.12.22
	}

	desc = "EVTDESC33408"
	picture = "ITAevent33408"

		name = "Let's proceed."
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		OMG = {
			any_country = {
				limit = { tag = ITA has_country_flag = BlackICE }
				set_country_flag = Ordinamento_Pariani
				set_country_flag = Ordinamento_Pariani_Limitation
			}
		}
		OMG = {
			any_country = {
				limit = { tag = ITA NOT = { has_country_flag = BlackICE } }
				set_country_flag = Ordinamento_Pariani	
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "Nonsense! We'll keep our 3 Regiments-sized divisions!"
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		officer_pool = 10000
	}
}

# Occupation of Albania

	fire_only_once = yes

		tag = ITA

		date = 1939.4.1
		not = { exists = ALB }
		money = 200
		metal = 500
		manpower = 30
		supplies = 8000

# Use of Chemical Weapons by Italy
country_event = {
	id = 33456

	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {
		tag = ITA
		date = 1936.3.1
		supplies = 1000
	}
	
	title = "EVTNAME33456"
	desc = "EVTDESC33456"
	picture = "ITAevent33456"
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA33456" #Let's use these chemical weapons!"

		OMG = {
			any_country = {
				limit = { tag = ITA has_country_flag = BlackICE }
				set_country_flag = Chemical_Weapons
				add_country_modifier = {
				name = "Chemical_Weapons"
				duration = 60
				}
			}
		}
		OMG = {
			any_country = {
				limit = { tag = ITA NOT = { has_country_flag = BlackICE } }
				set_country_flag = Chemical_Weapons
				add_country_modifier = {
				name = "Chemical_Weapons"
				duration = 60
				}
			}
		}
		supplies = -1000
		relation = { who = ENG value = -10 }
		relation = { who = FRA value = -10 }	
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
	
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB33456" #Hell no! I don't want to provocate England!"
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		relation = { who = ENG value = 5 }
		relation = { who = FRA value = 5 }
	}
}
# Corpo Aereo Italiano (small italian airforce sent to Belgium during Battle of Britain) - ITA choice

	id = 33457

		tag = ITA
		year = 1940
		month = 9
		faction = axis
		GER = { war_with = ENG }
		2311 = { controller = { faction = axis } }
		2613 = { controller = { faction = axis } }
		not = { has_country_flag = foreign_luftwaffe_CAI }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen =  {
		days = 1
	}
	
	title = "EVTNAME33457"
	desc = "EVTDESC33457"
	picture = "ITAevent33457"
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA33457"
		manpower = -8
		supplies = -500
		officer_pool = -500
		GER = { country_event = 33458 }
		set_country_flag = foreign_luftwaffe_CAI
		ai_chance = { factor = 70 }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB33457"
		manpower = -8
		supplies = -500
		officer_pool = -500
		set_country_flag = foreign_luftwaffe_CAI

# Addis Abeba Massacre (Historically on 19 Feb 1937, though we will fire it after the fall of Ethiopia)

country_event = {
	id = 33460

	major = yes
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {
		tag = ITA
		date = 1936.1.1
		controls = 9943 #Addis Ababa
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen =  {
		days = 90 # must happen a few monthes after Italian annexation
	}
	
	title = "EVTNAME33460"
	desc = "EVTDESC33460"
	picture = "ITAevent33460"

	option = {
		name = "Graziani is wounded! Punish them!"
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		
		# Adjust relations with various European countries
		relation = { who = ENG value = -5 }
		relation = { who = FRA value = -5 }
		relation = { who = USA value = -5 }
		relation = { who = GER value = 5 }
		
		# Increase the partisan activity in certain Ethiopian locations
		random_owned = { limit = { is_core = ETH } create_revolt = 2 supplies = 100 }
		random_owned = { limit = { is_core = ETH } create_revolt = 1 supplies = 100 }
		random_owned = { limit = { is_core = ETH } create_revolt = 1 supplies = 100 }
	}
}

                        check_variable = { which = "BaseIC" value = 750 }
                        not = { check_variable = { which = "BaseIC" value = 800 } }
                }
                add_country_modifier = {
                    name = "40IC_Unit_spawn_penalty_750_IV"
                    duration = 250
                }	
                load_oob = ITA/ITA_MilMART_1939.txt
            }
        }
        OMG = {
            any_country = {
                limit = { tag = ITA has_country_flag = BlackICE
                        check_variable = { which = "BaseIC" value = 800 }
                }
                add_country_modifier = {
                    name = "40IC_Unit_spawn_penalty_800_IV"
                    duration = 250
                }	
                load_oob = ITA/ITA_MilMART_1939.txt
            }
        }
		
		OMG = {
			any_country = {
				limit = { tag = ITA NOT = { has_country_flag = BlackICE } }
				load_oob = ITA/ITA_MilMART_1939.txt
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = MilMART_raised
		manpower = -30
		supplies = -5000
		officer_pool = -5000
		metal = -1000
		# Coastal batteries manned by MilMART
		3696 = { coastal_fort = 3 } #Venezia
		3971 = { coastal_fort = 2 } #Genova
		4868 = { coastal_fort = 2 } #Brindisi
		4869 = { coastal_fort = 1 } #Taranto
		3972 = { coastal_fort = 2 } #La Spezia
		4658 = { coastal_fort = 2 } #Olbia - In fact batteries located in La Maddalena
		5331 = { coastal_fort = 2 } #Syracusa - In fact batteries located in Augusta
		5203 = { coastal_fort = 2 } #Reggio
		5236 = { coastal_fort = 2 } #Messina
		
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
	
	}

	}

		2613 = { controller = { faction = axis } }
		not = { has_country_flag = foreign_Betasom }
		not = { has_country_flag = foreign_Betasom_NO }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen =  {
		days = 1
	}

	desc = "EVTDESC33463"
	picture = "ITAevent33463"

## Ordering the Battleships 'Roma' and 'Impero'(Littorio-Class)
country_event = {
	id = 33484
	

	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {
		tag = ITA
		has_country_flag = ITA_historical_OOB_yes
		date = 1938.9.1
		manpower = 8
		metal = 3000
	}
	
	
	title = "EVTNAME33484"
	desc = "EVTDESC33484"
	picture = "ITAevent33485"
	
	option = {
		name = "Lay down those two ships!"
		set_country_flag = RN_Roma
		set_country_flag = RN_Impero
		ai_chance = { factor = 75 }
        OMG = {
			any_country = {
				limit = { tag = ITA has_country_flag = BlackICE }
				load_oob = ITA/ITA_Roma_Impero.txt
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "Roma_Imperio_spawn_penalty"
				duration = 750
			}	
		}
        OMG = {
			any_country = {
				limit = { tag = ITA not = { has_country_flag = BlackICE }
				}
				load_oob = ITA/ITA_Roma_Impero.txt
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "We should focus on smaller ships for escort duties..."
		ai_chance = { factor = 25 }
	}
}
